# Breaking Changes in the last four months 
* Additional Q&A about breaking changes can be found [here](./breaking-changes.md) 
* To ask a question about breaking changes [use this](https://aka.ms/ask/ibiza-breaking-change)  


## 8.16.0.5
<table><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9896588'>9896588</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9896588'>Require extension name in C# test framework and pass that in the Url</a><p></div><div><br></div><div>The C# test framework now requires a partner team email to be provided starting with version <span style="display:inline !important;">1.0.232.0</span>.&nbsp;&nbsp;</div><div><br></div><div><span style="display:inline !important;">** Expected Errors: **</span><br></div><div>If a partner team email is not provided, the C# test framework will throw an exception at runtime with a message similar to the following:</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &quot;A partner team email must be provided via environment variable or in your app.config file via the value 'PartnerTeamEmail'.&quot;<br></div><div><br></div><div>** Solution: **</div><div>The partner team email can be provided in 1 of 2 ways:</div><div><ol><li>&nbsp;The environment variable &quot;<span style="display:inline !important;">PartnerTeamEmail</span>&quot; can be set with the team's email.&nbsp; eg: in a command line &quot;SET <span style="display:inline !important;">PartnerTeamEmail</span>=myTeamEmail@microsoft.com&quot;</li><li>&nbsp;The configuration setting &quot;<span style="display:inline !important;">PartnerTeamEmail</span>&quot; can be set in the app.config.&nbsp; eg:&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;add key=&quot;PartnerTeamEmail&quot; value=&quot;<span style="display:inline !important;">myTeamEmail</span>@microsoft.com&quot; /&gt;</li></ol><div>If both are provided, the environment variable will take precedence.</div></div><div><br></div><div>** Reason for Breaking Change**</div><div><br></div><div>The email is required so that we can correlate the incoming test traffic telemetry with the their team owners.&nbsp;&nbsp;</div><div><br></div><div><span style="display:inline !important;"></p></td></tr></table>

## 8.13.0.5

## 8.7.0.5
<table><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9849043'>9849043</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9849043'>[AzurePortal-Test] Require extension name in msportalfx-test config and pass that in the Url</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Expected Errors:<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">- When running azureportal-tests (formerly msportalfx-test), the PortalConfigurationManager class will throw a runtime error `No partner team name has been provided! The name can be specified as '--partnerTeam' argument, 'partnerTeam' environment variable or 'partnerTeam' field in config.json. For details see https://aka.ms/portalfx/e2e-testing#partner-team-name`<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Solution:<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">- If you receive this error, follow instructions in the error message or see an example at https://aka.ms/portalfx/<span>e2e-testing#partner-team-name</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Reason For Breaking Change<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">- Having an ability to see a footprint of which team runs an extension test.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr></table>

## 8.5.0.5
<table><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=10044366'>10044366</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=10044366'>Deprecate JQuery Promise and Deferred helpers</a><p></div><div>JQuery Promise and Deferred helpers are being deprecated in the Portal framework.&nbsp; Please switch to native promises.</div><div><br></div><div><div>MsPortalFx.Helpers.Deferred --&nbsp; Use defer() from the &quot;Fx&quot; module.<br></div><div><span>MsPortalFx.Helpers.resolve -- Use Promise.resove().</span><br></div><div><span>MsPortalFx.Helpers.reject -- Use Promise.reject().</span><br></div><div><span><br></span></div><div><span>The JQuery helpers are being deprecated and eventually removed.&nbsp; JQuery promises are non-standard.&nbsp; For consistent behavior and better performance extensions should use native promises.</span></div><div><span></p></td></tr></table>

## 8.2.0.5

instead.<div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason for Breaking Change**</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.SpecComparisonTable&nbsp;</span>is no longer supported. The&nbsp;<span style="box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, Arial, Verdana, sans-serif;text-align:left;display:inline !important;">viewModel<span style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</span><span style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:start;display:inline !important;">and its associated types have</span>&nbsp;been obsoleted in the May2021 breaking SDK release. Please use&nbsp;Fx/Controls/DataGrid, Fx/Controls/EditableGrid&nbsp;<span style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:start;display:inline !important;">which use AMD imports that improves Portal performance.</span></span><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;">OptionsWithBladeReference</span></div><div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div !important;">DropDown</span></div></span></div></span></div></div></div><br></div><div><span>**Solution:** Please use Fx/Controls/</span><span>DropDown</span><span> instead. Pickers in general are an older pattern that has been replaced by the new create experience with tabs and drop-downs, e.g. samples at </span><a href="https://na01.safelinks.protection.outlook.com/?url=https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/%23blade/SamplesExtension/CreateLauncherBlade&amp;data=02%7c01%7c%7cf2125bd1230f46e16f7008d5fd7c6d5e%7c72f988bf86f141af91ab2d7cd011db47%7c1%7c0%7c636693633195780929&amp;sdata=jREtfQ1XFvbFv58jjMtJmntUFKs78kjGCNM7tVofbms%3D&amp;reserved=0"><span style="font-size:12.0pt;">https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/#blade/SamplesExtension/CreateLauncherBlade</span></a><span>.</span><br></div><div><br></div><div>**Reason For Breaking Change:** This control is part of an old pattern as described above.<br></div><div><br></div><div></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9856512'>9856512</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9856512'>DEPRECATE: MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Lists.TreeView</a><p></div><div>MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Lists.TreeView has been deprecated.&nbsp; You should encounter deprecation errors when compiling if you are using this control.<br></div><div><br></div><div>Instances of this control can be replaced with the &quot;Fx/Controls/TreeView&quot; control.&nbsp; The AMD control works similarly to the old control but with slightly enhanced contracts and options.&nbsp; The full details of the new API are in intellisense supplied by the Fx.d.ts file from your SDK.&nbsp; However, you can also see the API here:</div><div><br></div><blockquote style="margin:0 0 0 40px;border:none;"><div><a href="https://msazure.visualstudio.com/One/_git/AzureUX-PortalFx?path=/src/SDK/Framework.Client/TypeScript/Fx/Controls/TreeView.ts&amp;version=GBproduction&amp;_a=contents">https://msazure.visualstudio.com/One/_git/AzureUX-PortalFx?path=%2Fsrc%2FSDK%2FFramework.Client%2FTypeScript%2FFx%2FControls%2FTreeView.ts&amp;version=GBproduction&amp;_a=contents</a></div></blockquote><div><br></div><div>The following short descriptions of the changes should help converting to the new control:.</div><div><ul><li><span>Control is now imported as an AMD module from &quot;Fx/Controls/TreeView&quot;.</span></li><li><span>The control is created with a &quot;create&quot; function instead of constructor.</span></li><li><span>Instead of a ViewModel the control has a Contract.</span></li><li><span>&quot;ExtensionsOptions&quot; interface was renamed to &quot;Options&quot;.</span></li><li>&quot;Extensions&quot; enum and bit flags were removed. Instead setting an option enables it.</li><li>The &quot;extensions&quot; and &quot;extensionsOptions&quot; properties were removed from the contract.</li><li>The &quot;items&quot; constructor param was changed to an option.</li><li>The following internal options/properties were removed from public view &quot;loadingPath&quot;, &quot;syncToken&quot;, &quot;toggleNodeCallback&quot;.</li><li>New options were added tor &quot;htmlTemplates&quot; and &quot;pathSeparator&quot; and the corresponding contract properties were removed.</li><li>All promises were changed to native &quot;Promise&quot; type (You can still use Q if you want because it now extends native Promise in the framework).</li><li>The &quot;supplyCommands&quot; option was moved from &quot;selection&quot; to &quot;contextMenu&quot;.</li><li>Toolbar types where changed to &quot;Fx/Controls/Toolbar&quot; types.</li><li>The &quot;commandGroup&quot; property was removed from the item contract.</li><li>The &quot;TSelection&quot; generic type was removed along with the &quot;createSelection&quot; callback. Instead we have a fixed &quot;SelectedItem&quot; type that includes the item and path.</li><li>The &quot;selectableData&quot; property and types were removed. Instead we have two properties on the contract &quot;selectedPaths&quot; which gets or sets the current selection and &quot;selectedItems&quot; that returns the current selection. These work for both single and multiple selection.</li><li>The &quot;initialPath&quot; option was removed. It was a strange option that only worked in single select. Setting the &quot;selectedPaths&quot; before the widget is created is equivalent.</li><li>Added readonly to properties where applicable.&nbsp; Initial values should be set through options now.</li><li><span>readonly was added to Item and Metadata properties.&nbsp; This may require you to construct the properties all at once.</span><br></li><li><span>rightClick renamed to contextMenu</span><br></li><li>onDemandLoadable renamed to deferredLoading</li><li>loadByContinuationToken renamed sequentialLoading</li><li>loadMoreNode renamed loadMoreChildItems</li><li>added canLoadMoreRootItems option</li></ul></div><div><span>The UI rendering for the TreeView has not been modified.&nbsp; All existing test harnesses that manipulate the UI should continue to work without change.</span></div><div><span></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9856502'>9856502</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9856502'>DEPRECATE: MsPortalFx.ViewModels.ClickableLink</a><p></span><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:** <span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.ClickableLink is MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.SingleSetting</a><p></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">The obsolete MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.SingleSetting control has been removed from the product.&nbsp; This control was obsoleted in 2018 and should no longer be in use.&nbsp; If you are still using it your blade will fail.&nbsp; Blades must be modified to use custom html instead.<br Please use the native Promise type directly instead of this alias.</div><div><span style=""></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9390560'>9390560</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9390560'>Add HtmlContent to properly support html rendering</a><p></div><div>Before this change, several framework APIs remained that allowed html to be provided through a string-typed 'text' property.&nbsp; This is a risk for html injection.&nbsp; The framework has been logging errors to extensions to fix these but in a few cases there was not an actionable way to do so.&nbsp; Breaking changes to these remaining APIs have been made to allow extensions to properly specify html and avoid html injection.</div><div><br></div><div>The following APIs now allow HtmlContent in addition to string text.</div><div><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; ValidationResult message</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; StaticMessageValidation message</div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; NotRegExMatchValidation successMessage</div><div><span style="display:inline !important;">&nbsp; &nbsp; RegExMatchValidation successMessage</span><br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; InfoBox text</div><div><span></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9219252'>9219252</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9219252'>Deprecate Q APIs that  no longer do anything or are not needed</a><p></div><div>Some Q APIs that are no longer applicable to the Portal have been deprecated.&nbsp; Some previously deprecated types have been removed. In addition some Q API signatures have changed to enhance type safety.&nbsp; Also, some diagnostic APIs that used deprecated Q APIs have been deprecated.</div><div><br></div><div><span><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.</span>IPromise - Removed. Use PromiseLike instead.</span><br></div><div><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.</span>QPromiseLike - Removed. Use PromiseLike instead.</div><div><br></div><div><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.Promise </span>fin&nbsp; - Deprecated. Use finally instead</div><div><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.Promise </span>fail - Deprecated. Use catch instead.</div><div><br></div><div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Q.longStackSupport - Deprecated. No longer does anything in the portal.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.</span>getUnhandledRejections - Deprecated. No longer does anything in the portal.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.</span>getUnhandledReasons - Deprecated. No longer does anything in the portal.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.</span>resetUnhandledRejections - Deprecated. No longer does anything in the portal.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">MsPortalFx.Base.Diagnostics.</span><span>setPromiseErrorCapturePeriod - Deprecated. No longer does anything.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span><span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.Base.Diagnostics.</span>clearPromiseErrorCaptureTimeout - Deprecated. No longer does anything.</span></div><br></div><div><span><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.</span>isPromise - Enhanced type safety with type guard.</span><br></div><div><span style="display:inline !important;">Q.</span>isPromiseAlike&nbsp;<span style="display:inline !important;"><span>&nbsp;</span>- Enhanced type safety with type guard.</span></div><div><span style="display:inline !important;"><br></span></div><div>Previously, Q Promise was changed to extend the native Promise.&nbsp; With this change unhandled rejections are now managed in the Portal using the native browser mechanisms. specifies the old type.<br></div><div><br></div><div>**Reason For Breaking Change:** Extension devs expressed desires to be able to provide computed observables too for said `disabled` options.<br></div><div><br></div><span></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=10004261'>10004261</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=10004261'>Upgrade Portal SDK to TypeScript 4.2</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">The tooling was updated to use TypeScript 4.2 (update from TypeScript 4.1).<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">There were no Portal-specific changes required by this upgrade, but the tooling update itself might cause some breaks in extension code.</span><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">See breaking changes and changelog in the official TypeScript site: <a href="https://github.com/Microsoft/TypeScript/wiki/Breaking-Changes">https://github.com/Microsoft/TypeScript/wiki/Breaking-Changes</a></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">In addition, the npm dependencies for `@microsoft/eslint-plugin-azureportal` were updated to support the new syntax in TypeScript 4.2 (in particular, we updated all the packages in the `@typescript-eslint` scope).</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Although extensions using ReactViews are compiled using the version of the compiler in the `@microsoft/azureportal-reactview-tools` npm package (TypeScript 3.9 as of 0.13.0), the Portal SDK was compiling the react view code using its own TypeScript compiler version (and then discarding the results, as part of a side-effect of the Ibiza precompilation process). Because of this, there might be some TypeScript 4.2 related errors coming from this process in the Error output stream. If that is the case, please update to&nbsp;<span style="display:inline !important;">`@microsoft/azureportal-reactview-tools`<span>&nbsp;version 0.15.0 or newer, which should resolve this double-compilation. Alternatively (if can't update the tools package yet), set the `listFilesOnly` flag to `true` in the tsconfig.json file that corresponds to the extension using ReactViews (in the `compilerOptions` section).</span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;"><span><br></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;"><span><span>A common example of this double-compilation issue might be if your build shows the following in the following in the Error output stream:<br></span><div>```<br></div><div>error TS2343: Build:This syntax requires an imported helper named '__spreadArray' which does not exist in 'tslib'. Consider upgrading your version of 'tslib'.<br></div><span>```</span><br></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=10003350'>10003350</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=10003350'>renavigateActivatedBlade is obsolete</a><p></span><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">The SDK API renavigateActivedBlade is obsolete.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;font-size:10.5pt;color:black;">**Expected Errors:**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;font-size:10.5pt;color:black;"></p><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"></span></span></div>error TS2349: Build:This expression is not callable.<div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></span></div><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;font-size:10.5pt;color:black;">**Solution:**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;font-size:10.5pt;color:black;">Change the extension code to use openBlade instead.</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;"><font face="Segoe UI VSS (Regular)" style="box-sizing:border-box;"></font></p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;font-size:10.5pt;color:black;">**Reason For Breaking Change**</p></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">This API is obsolete and is being retired.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"></p></td></tr></table>

## 7.289.0.5
<table><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9867718'>9867718</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9867718'>Remove obsoleted nuget packages; create samples extension/internal samples extension packages</a><p></div><div>**Expected errors**</div><div>Two obsolete NuGet packages are being removed as part of this change. Anyone still depending on them will break their build.</div><div><br></div><div>**Solution**</div><div>If the files are found in another Azure Portal SDK NuGet package, please use that.</div><div>If the files are not found elsewhere, and you have not migrated to the Hosting Service, please do that migration.</div><div>If the files are not found and you have already migrated, please contact the Azure Portal team to identify the files used and why.</div><div><br></div><div>**Reason for breaking change**</div><div>These packages have been marked obsolete since 2019. We are making some build system changes internal to the Portal's build and removing these projects is part of that process.</div><div><br></div><div></p></td></tr></table>

## 7.38.0.5
<table><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9070831'>9070831</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=9070831'>Update EHS version to be semver</a><p><br></span><div><br></div><div>Expected Issue:<br></div><div>- Wont pick up latest version of @microsoft/portalhostingservice<br></div><div><br></div><div>Solution:<br></div><div>- update reference of @microsoft/portalhostingservice in package.json<br></div><div><br></div><div>```<br></div><div>before:<br></div><div>{<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; devDependencies: {<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &quot;@microsoft/portalhostingservice&quot;: &quot;1.182.*&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; }<br></div><div>}<br></div><div><br></div><div>after:<br></div><div>{<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; devDependencies: {<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &quot;@microsoft/portalhostingservice&quot;: &quot;^1.182.0&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; }<br></div><div>}<br></div><div><br></div><div>```<br></div><div><br></div><div>Reason For Breaking Change:<br></div><div>- alignment of versioning to industry standard practises or using SemVer.<br></div><div><br></div><div></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8966771'>8966771</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8966771'>Require that MsPortalFx.d.ts be the same version as the SDK</a><p></span></p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">**Expected Errors:**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">- You may see a error like this when compiling your extension:&nbsp;error TS2339: Build:Property 'Version' does not exist on type 'typeof MsPortalFx'.</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">**Solution:**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">- You have a version of MsPortalFx.d.ts checked in that is older or doesn't match the version of the SDK you are using.</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">**Reason For Breaking Change**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">- Some partner teams have been checking older versions of MsPortalFx.d.ts into their repositories.&nbsp; In some cases this can cause runtime breaks if the extension code is using obsolete features.&nbsp; &nbsp;We have added a compile time check to ensure the copy of MsPortalFx.d.ts that is being used matches the current SDK version.</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;background:white;"></p></td></tr></table>

## 7.16.0.5
<table><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8966771'>8966771</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8966771'>Require that MsPortalFx.d.ts be the same version as the SDK</a><p></span></p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">**Expected Errors:**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">- You may see a error like this when compiling your extension:&nbsp;error TS2339: Build:Property 'Version' does not exist on type 'typeof MsPortalFx'.</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">**Solution:**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">- You have a version of MsPortalFx.d.ts checked in that is older or doesn't match the version of the SDK you are using.</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">**Reason For Breaking Change**</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;">- Some partner teams have been checking older versions of MsPortalFx.d.ts into their repositories.&nbsp; In some cases this can cause runtime breaks if the extension code is using obsolete features.&nbsp; &nbsp;We have added a compile time check to ensure the copy of MsPortalFx.d.ts that is being used matches the current SDK version.</p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;font-size:10.5pt;margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;background:white;"></p></td></tr></table>

style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;">- error TS2322: Build:Type 'Promise&lt;any&gt;' is not assignable to type 'Q.Promise&lt;any&gt;'.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span Promise&lt;any&gt;';</p><p style="margin:0in;font-size:10.5pt;color:black;"><span><font face="Segoe UI VSS (Regular)">- I</font></span><span>f you need a Q feature that is not supported by native browser promises you may wrap the result returned from ajax with Q().</span></p><p style="margin:0in;"><font face="Segoe UI VSS (Regular)"></font></p><p style="margin:0in;">&nbsp;</p><p promise implementations that have better error handling and performance.&nbsp; The SDK is standardizing on native promises wherever possible.</div><div><span style="display:inline href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8827920'>Remove armEndpointLowerCase from Fx/Ajax</a><p><br></div><div>&nbsp;<br></div><div>**Expected Errors:**<br></div><div>&nbsp;- Expect compile-time errors when using armEndpointLowerCase from the Fx/Ajax module<br></div><div>&nbsp;<br></div><div>**Solution:**<br></div><div>&nbsp;-

 commonly-used endpoints, and lowercase the `arm` property if necessary<br></div><div>&nbsp;<br></div><div>**Reason For Breaking Change**<br></div><div>&nbsp;- Unnecessary duplication with getEndpoints()<br></div><div><br></div><div></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8819863'>8819863</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8819863'>SDK: container.helpContentUri is obsolete</a><p></div><div><span>**Expected Errors:**</span><br></div><div><span>&nbsp;error TS2349: This expression is not callable.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span>Type 'Obsolete' has no call signatures.</span><br></div><div><div><span>120 &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; container.helpContentUri</span><br></div></div><div><span><br></span></div><div><span>**Solution:**</span></div><div><span>Remove the line of code that references the property.&nbsp;</span></div><div><span><br></span></div><div><span>**Reason For Breaking Change:**</span></div><div><span>This API has been removed.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span>There is no replacement or substitute.</span></div><div></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8807165'>8807165</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8807165'>Make Q.Promise extend native Promise</a><p></div><div>The Q.Promise implementation in the Portal Framework has been updated to subclass the native Promise.&nbsp; APIs returning Q.Promise may now be typed to return native Promise. Interfaces QPromiseLike and IPromise have been deprecated.</div><div><br></div><div><span style="">Extensions could experience compile errors where Q.Promises are expected.&nbsp; To resolve these issues quickly promises can be converted to Q.Promise by wrapping with Q().&nbsp; Longer term extensions could use adopt native Promise.</span><br></div><div><span><br></span></div><div><span>Extensions may also get deprecation warnings if using QPromiseLike or IPromise types.&nbsp; These type can be replaced with the PromiseLike interface.&nbsp; The PromiseLike interface is a global type that is included with the TypeScript library and can be used without importing a module.</span></div><div><span style=""></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8752127'>8752127</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8752127'>Enable native Promise on all Grid2 APIs</a><p></span></div><div>To improve performance the Portal framework is standardizing on native Promises.&nbsp; When the Portal was created it used JQuery Promises and then later adapted to Q Promises.&nbsp; We now have native Promises or pollyfills in all browsers. TypeScript includes definitions for Promise and support for async/await using them.&nbsp; The native Promises are faster and standard so the Portal is in the process of transitioning APIs to use them.</div><div><br></div><div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">To help aid in this process the Q.Promise implementation in the Portal framework is now type and run-time compatible with native Promises.<span style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</span><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">This means that you can continue to pass Q.Promise to APIs that are now typed Promise without error. For APIs that used to return Q.Promise and now return Promise you can wrap the return value with Q() as required.&nbsp; In both cases you now have the option of removing Q.Promise and using native Promises.</span></div><br><span style="">The following grid APIs for &quot;Fx/Controls/DataGrid&quot; and &quot;Fx/Controls/EditableGrid&quot; have been changed:</span><br></div><div><span><br></span></div><div><span>getChildren<br></span><div>supplyButtonCommands<br></div><div>supplyMenuBulkCommands<br></div><div>supplyMenuCommands<br></div><div>collapseRow<br></div><div>expandRow<br></div><div>displayLoadingMessage<br></div><div>refresh<br></div><div>triggerValidation<br></div><div>canStopEditingRow<br></div><div>stopEditingRow<br></div><div>validateAsync<br></div><div><span style=""><br></span></div><div><span style=""></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716828'>8716828</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716828'> Mark Gallery as obsolete</a><p></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="">If you are using the MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Lists.Gallery control you will get compile errors that it is obsolete.</span><br></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style=""><br></span></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="">To resolve these you can switch to using Fx/Controls/ListView control in gallery mode.</span></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style=""><br></span></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="">The gallery control is a non-AMD control and is loaded in every extension at startup even when it is not being used.&nbsp; Moving to the AMD ListView will allow it to be loaded on demand.&nbsp; The Gallery control has been deprecated previously.&nbsp; So most extensions should have already made the requested change.</span></p><span style="display:inline !important;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716813'>8716813</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716813'>Deprecate SpecComparisonTable control</a><p></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;">If you are using MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.SpecComparisonTable you will get compile errors that it has been deprecated.</p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><br></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;">This should be addressed by using alternate UI for comparing specs.&nbsp; If desired to use similar UI a custom table can be generated using custom html.</p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><br></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;">The&nbsp;<span style="display:inline !important;">SpecComparisonTable is not an AMD module and is currently loaded into every extension.&nbsp; The control is only used in a handful of scenarios.&nbsp; To reduce memory for all extensions this control is being removed.</span></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="font-weight:inherit;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716806'>8716806</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716806'>Deprecate QueryBuilder control</a><p></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;">You will experience compilation errors when using the QueryBuilder control indicating that the control is deprecated.</p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><br></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="">If you are using the QueryBuilder control you should migrate to a newer experience.&nbsp; One option is to make a customized experience using the EditableGrid.&nbsp; Another option is to use an Editor for directly modifying queries.</span><br></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style=""><br></span></p><p style="margin:0in;color:black;"><span style=""><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;color:black;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Data.QueryBuilder</span> is one of the few remaining non-AMD controls .&nbsp; Currently all extensions must load this even though there are very few that use it.&nbsp; The control is being deprecated now and will eventually be removed.</span></p><p style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0in;color:black;"><span style=""></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716780'>8716780</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716780'> Mark iFrame as obsolete</a><p></span><br></p></div><div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">You will hit compilation error when using <span>MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Internal.Iframe</span><span>.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span>MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Internal.Iframe types were deprecated in May 2020.&nbsp; In the November 2020 breaking SDK release, this has</span></span><span>&nbsp;been marked as obsolete.&nbsp; The API will be deleted in the next breaking SDK release (2021).</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please migrate to the new AMD API in Fx/Controls/FrameControl<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Eg.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">import * as FrameControl from &quot;Fx/Controls/FrameControl&quot;;<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">const frameControl = FrameControl.create(container, {<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; src: &quot;MyIFrameUri&quot;,<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; onReceiveMessage: (message) =&gt; {<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // Handle messages from Iframe window.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; },</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">});</span></div></div><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at playground sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground</a></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at SDK sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls</a></div><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">MsPortalFx namespace is a non-AMD module. For perf reasons we have exposed new AMD modules under Fx/Controls and asking partners to migrate to new API patterns.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please refer to https://aka.ms/portalfx/breaking for more details.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716751'>8716751</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716751'>  Mark infobox as obsolete</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:** Usage of the old InfoBox view models and options (i.e. <span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.InfoBox.ViewModel,<span>&nbsp;</span></span><span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.InfoBox.BaseViewModel,<span>&nbsp;<span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.InfoBox.LinkViewModel,<span>&nbsp;<span style="display:inline !important;"><span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.InfoBox.<span style="display:inline !important;">LinkInfoBoxOptions</span>,</span><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</span></span></span></span></span></span></span>and&nbsp;MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.<span style="display:inline !important;">InfoBox.BaseInfoBoxOptions</span>) will be flagged as a compile-time typescript errors at build time:<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change:**<span>&nbsp;</span>This control has accessibility issues and is an old pattern of creating links.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716558'>8716558</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716558'>Breaking changes- Deprecate metrics from Codebase</a><p></span><br></p></div><div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">You will hit tslint errors when using <span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Visualization.Metrics</span> view model.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Visualization.Metrics types are deprecated</span>&nbsp;in the November 2020 breaking SDK release,&nbsp;</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">If Metrics is used as part of MsPortalFx Chart or Donut/Gauge parts add tslint comment to disable the warning -&nbsp;</span><span style="display:inline !important;">// tslint:disable:deprecation</span><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please migrate MsPortalFx Chart to Fx/Controls/LineChart or <span style="display:inline !important;">Fx/Controls/</span>BarChart or <span style="display:inline !important;">Fx/Controls/</span>AreaChart or <span style="display:inline !important;">Fx/Controls/</span>ScatterChart.&nbsp;</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;"><br></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">If Metrics is used as a standalone control, p<span style="font-weight:inherit;">lease migrate to the new AMD API in Fx/Controls/Metrics.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Eg.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span>import * as SingleMetric from &quot;Fx/Controls/SingleMetric&quot;;<br></span><span>import * as Metrics from &quot;Fx/Controls/Metrics&quot;;</span><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span><div><br></div><div>const metricItem = SingleMetric.create(container, {<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; caption: &quot;myCaption&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; unit: &quot;myUnit&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; value: &quot;myValue&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; hatchingPattern: SingleMetric.Pattern.DottedHatching,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; showBarColor: true,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; barCssClass: SingleMetric.FxChartColorClass.Color2,</div><div><span style="font-weight:inherit;">});</span></div></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span><br></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span>const metrics = Metrics.create(container, {<br></span><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ariaLabel: &quot;aria-label for the whole metrics control&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; items: [<span style="display:inline !important;">metricItem</span><span style="font-weight:inherit;">],</span></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; orientation: Metrics.Orientation.Horizontal,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; size: Metrics.Size.Small,</div><div><span style="font-weight:inherit;">});</span></div></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span><br></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at playground sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground</a></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at SDK sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls</a></div><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx namespace is a non-AMD module. For perf reasons</span>&nbsp;we have exposed AMD modules under Fx/Controls and asking partners to migrate to new API patterns.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please refer to https://aka.ms/portalfx/breaking for more details.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716525'>8716525</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716525'>Breaking changes- obsolete asyncfileupload from Codebase</a><p></span><br></p><div style="margin:0px 0in;color:black;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">You will hit compilation error when using <span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Forms.AsyncFileUpload view model</span>.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Forms.AsyncFileUpload</span>&nbsp;types are marked as obsolete in the November 2020 breaking SDK release.&nbsp;</span><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">The API will be deleted in the next breaking SDK release (2021).</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please migrate to the new AMD API in Fx/Controls/FileUpload<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Eg.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">import * as FileUpload from &quot;Fx/Controls/FileUpload&quot;;<br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span>const fileUpload = FileUpload.createBlobStoreUpload(container, {</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="font-weight:inherit;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; label: &quot;myLabel&quot;,</span><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; infoBalloonContent: &quot;myInfoBaloonContent&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; placeHolderText: &quot;Select a file&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; uploadContext: new FileUpload.BlobStoreFileUploadContext({<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; type:FileUpload.UploadType.BlockBlobStore ,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; category: &quot;SampleUploads&quot;,<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; authorizationContext: {<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; fetchAuthorization: (_fileInfo, _context) =&gt; {<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // Return SAS uri or auth token. <br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; },<br></div><div>&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; },</div><div><span style="font-weight:inherit;">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }),</span></div><div><span style="font-weight:inherit;">});</span></div><div><span style="font-weight:inherit;"><br></span></div><span></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at playground sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground</a></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at SDK sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls</a></div><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">MsPortalFx namespace is a non-AMD module. For perf reasons we have exposed new AMD modules under Fx/Controls and asking partners to migrate to new API patterns.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please refer to https://aka.ms/portalfx/breaking for more details.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716497'>8716497</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716497'>Breaking changes- Delete image API  from Codebase</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">If using an icon that has been removed, you will get a building with wording similar to &quot;This expression is not callable&quot;.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Use the following table to find a replacement for your icon:</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><table width=621 style="border-collapse:collapse;width:466pt;">

  <td width=337 style="padding-top:1px;padding-right:1px;padding-left:1px;color:black;font-size:11pt;font-family:Calibri, sans-serif;vertical-align:bottom;border:none;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, sans-serif;vertical-align:middle;border-top:1pt solid rgb(163, 163, 163);border-right:none;border-bottom:1pt solid rgb(163, 163, 163);border-left:1pt solid rgb(163, 163, 163);background:white;border:1px solid rgb(212, 212, 212);border-top:none;border-left:none;width:253pt;font-size:11.0pt;border:1.0pt solid #A3A3A3;background:white</p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716472'>8716472</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716472'>Breaking changes- Delete infobox (image) API  from Codebase</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;margin:0px 0in;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:** Usage of 'image'&nbsp;<span style="display:inline !important;">option</span>&nbsp;in Fx/Controls/InfoBox<span>&nbsp;</span>is now runtime-breaking after over 6 months of getting flagged as a compile-time typescript error at build time.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:**<span>&nbsp;</span><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">&nbsp;</span></span>Custom images are no longer supported for InfoBoxes. Only the prebuilt styles are supported.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change:** This is the last stage of cleaning the Fx InfoBox API from the legacy fields prior to its Fluent UI redesign.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716458'>8716458</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716458'>Breaking changes- Delete infobox API  from Codebase</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="margin:0px 0in;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:** Usage of 'size'&nbsp;<span style="display:inline !important;">option</span> in Fx/Controls/InfoBox is now runtime-breaking after over 6 months of getting flagged as a compile-time typescript error at build time.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:** <span style="display:inline !important;"><span>&nbsp;</span>Extensions
should choose between '<span style="font-weight:bold;">create</span>' and '<span style="font-weight:bold;">createInline</span>' to differentiate between the 2
modes</span>.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change:** This is the last stage of cleaning the Fx InfoBox API from the legacy fields prior to its Fluent UI redesign.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span><br></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716414'>8716414</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716414'>Breaking changes- Delete Tooltip API  from Codebase</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">You will hit runtime errors when using 'tooltip' property for Pill in Fx/Controls/Pill.<span>&nbsp;</span><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;">The Pill's tooltip property was obsoleted in May 2020 SDK release and the property has been completely deleted in November 2020 breaking SDK release.</span><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please migrate to 'infoBalloonContent' property for Pill to show tooltip.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at playground sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://aka.ms/portalfx/playground</a></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please take a look at SDK sample @&nbsp;<a href="https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls" style="box-sizing:border-box;text-decoration:underline;cursor:pointer;">https://df.onecloud.azure-test.net/?SamplesExtension=true#blade/SamplesExtension/SDKMenuBlade/controls</a></div><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">'tooltip' property was using Balloon view model from MsPortalFx namespace which is a non-AMD module. For perf reasons we have exposed AMD modules under Fx/Controls and asking partners to migrate to new API patterns. We have removed all dependencies on MsPortalFx from AMD modules under Fx/Controls/.&nbsp;<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716390'>8716390</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716390'>Breaking changes- Delete QuotaGauge code from Codebase</a><p></span><br></div><div><br></div><div>**Expected Errors:**<br></div><div>You will hit runtime errors when using MsPortalFx view models for the below controls. <br></div><div><br></div><div>MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Visualization.Donut<br></div><div>MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Visualization.QuotaGauge<br></div><div>MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Visualization.SingleValueGauge<br></div><div><br></div><div>These MsPortalFx view models were obsoleted in May 2020 SDK release and these MsPortalFx view models are completely deleted in November 2020 breaking SDK release.<br></div><div><br></div><div>**Solution:**<br></div><div>Please migrate to the new AMD modules in Fx/Controls/<br></div><div>Fx/Controls/Donut<br></div><div>Fx/Controls/QuotaGauge<br></div><div>Fx/Controls/SingleValueGauge<br></div><div><br></div><div>Eg.&nbsp;</div><div>import * as Donut from &quot;Fx/Controls/Donut&quot;;<br></div><div><br></div><div><span>const donut = Donut.create(container, {<br></span><div>&nbsp; style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change**<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx namespace is a non-AMD module. For perf reasons</span>&nbsp;we have exposed AMD modules under Fx/Controls and asking partners to migrate to new API patterns.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Please refer to https://aka.ms/portalfx/breaking for more details.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716339'>8716339</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716339'>Breaking changes- Delete diffeditor code from Codebase</a><p>&nbsp;</div><div style="font-weight:400;box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:**</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, Arial, Verdana, sans-serif;"><ul style="box-sizing:border-box;padding:0px 0px 0px 40px;"><li style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">You will hit compilation error stating that&nbsp; <span style="font-weight:700;text-align:start;display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Documents.DiffEditor</span>&nbsp;does not exist (or related <span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, Arial, Verdana, sans-serif;text-align:start;display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Documents.DiffEditor.</span>Options, <span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, Arial, Verdana, sans-serif;text-align:start;display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Documents.DiffEditor.</span>Contract,&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, Arial, Verdana, sans-serif;text-align:start;display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Documents.DiffEditor.</span>ViewModel)&nbsp;</span></li></ul></span></div><div style="font-weight:400;box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution**</div><div style="font-weight:400;box-sizing:border-box;">You should use Fx/Controls/DiffEditor instead.</div><div style="font-weight:400;box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="font-weight:400;box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason for Breaking Change**</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.Documents.DiffEditor</span><span style="font-weight:400;">&nbsp;is no longer supported. The&nbsp;<span style="box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, Arial, Verdana, sans-serif;text-align:left;display:inline !important;">viewModel has been deleted in the November 2020 breaking SDK release. It has been replaced with&nbsp;<span style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:start;display:inline !important;">Fx/Controls/<span style="display:inline !important;">DiffEditor</span>, which uses AMD imports that improves Portal performance.</span></span><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="font-weight:400;box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Web&quot;, Arial, Verdana, sans-serif;text-align:left;display:inline !important;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:start;display:inline !important;"></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716328'>8716328</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8716328'>Breaking changes- Delete simplebutton code from Codebase</a><p><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Expected Errors:** usage of the old SimpleButton view model and options (i.e. MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.<span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"></span>SimpleButton<span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;">.ViewModel</span>&nbsp;and MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.<span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"></span>SimpleButton<span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;">.Options</span>) is now runtime-breaking after over 6 months of getting flagged as a compile-time typescript error at build time.<br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">Additionally, the went three types that went along have also been removed:&nbsp;MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.SimpleButton.Image, MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.SimpleButton.IconPosition, and MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Controls.SimpleButton.IconAndPosition, and using either of the three is compile-time breaking too.</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solution:** Please use Fx/Controls/Button&nbsp;<span control. For perf reasons we have exposed new AMD modules under Fx/Controls and asking partners to migrate to new API patterns.</span></span></span></p><div style="box-sizing:border-box;text-align:start;">Please refer to https://aka.ms/portalfx/breaking for more details.</div><p></p><p lang=EN-US options (i.e. <span style="display:inline !important;">MsPortalFx.ViewModels.Forms.</span><span style="box-sizing:border-box;display:inline !important;"></span><span style="display:inline MsPortalFx.Base.Promise ES6 compliant</a><p></div><div><span>**Expected Errors:**</span><br></div><div><br></div><div>- error TS2339: Property 'progress' does not exist on type 'Promise'.<br></div><div><br></div><div>**Solution:**</div><div><br></div><div>- It is recommend to develop a alternate solution for reporting progress.&nbsp; Alternatively you may wrap the promise with Q though this is less performant than using browser provided promise implementation.&nbsp;&nbsp;<span>i.e. Q(promise).progress(..</span></div><div><br></div><div>**Reason For Breaking Change**</div><div><br></div><div>The native promise implementation provided by browsers is more performant than Q promises.&nbsp; The portal team is changing the implementation of the SDK APIs to use native promises that conform to the ES6 promise specification.</div><div><br></div><div><span></p></td></tr><tr><td><a Emoji&quot;, sans-serif;"><span>&nbsp;- teams that require multiple node module registries need all of portals packages within the same scope i.e @microsoft so a scoped registry can be used in .npmrc.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, system-ui, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, sans-serif;"><span>- alignment of name to a scope for eventual public node module.</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&quot;Segoe UI&quot;, system-ui, &quot;Apple Color Emoji&quot;, &quot;Segoe UI Emoji&quot;, sans-serif;"><span></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8474147'>8474147</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8474147'>[msportalfx-test] Refactor ElementArrayFinder constructor params</a><p><br></div><div><div>&nbsp;</div><div>**Expected Errors:**</div><div><br></div><div>- You will hit the following compilation error for ElementArrayFinder usages that pass in parameters.</div></div><blockquote style="margin:0 0 0 40px;border:none;"><div><pre><code><div> error TS2554: Expected 0-1 arguments, but got 5.</div></code></pre></div></blockquote><div><div>**Solution:**</div><div>&nbsp;</div><div>- Convert ElementArrayFinder constructor parameters into an options object.</div><div>&nbsp;&nbsp;</div><div>&nbsp; Before:</div></div><blockquote style="margin:0 0 0 40px;border:none;"><div><div><pre><code><div>new ElementArrayFinder(this.getWebElements, this.elementLocator, undefined, undefined, this.frameId);</div></code></pre></div></div></blockquote><div><div>&nbsp; After:</div></div><blockquote style="margin:0 0 0 40px;border:none;"><pre><code><div><div><div>new ElementArrayFinder({</div></div></div><div><div>    getWebElements: this.getWebElements,</div></div><div><div>    locator: this.elementLocator,</div></div><div><div>    frameId: this.frameId,</div></div><div><div>});</div></div></code></pre></blockquote><div><div>**Reason For Breaking Change**</div><div>&nbsp;</div></div><div><div>- This refactor will eliminate the need to pass in undefined for optional parameters.</div></div><div><br></div><div><div></p></td></tr><tr><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8091023'>8091023</a></td><td><a href='https://msazure.visualstudio.com/DefaultCollection/One/_queries?id=8091023'>[BREAKING] Make the isTenantParityDependent property in MsPortalFx.Base.Security.UserInfo non-optional</a><p><br></div><div><br></div><div>**Expected Errors:**</div><div><br></div><div><ul><li>May see errors when using a mocked version of the &quot;MsPortalFx.Base.Security.UserInfo&quot; object without an &quot;isTenantParityDependent&quot; property as this property is now required. The error may be seen through intellisense as incomplete, or during compilation if that property is not present.</li></ul></div><div><span><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Solutions:**</div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><ul><li><span><div style="box-sizing:border-box;">If you encounter an error like this, simply add the &quot;<span style="display:inline !important;">isTenantParityDependent&quot;<span>&nbsp;property to your UserInfo mocks with a default value of false to have your tests perform exactly as they were before this change. The &quot;<span style="display:inline !important;">isTenantParityDependent&quot; is used internally by the portal during startup and should have no affect on extension code's use of the portal.</span></span></span></div></span></li></ul></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br style="box-sizing:border-box;">**Reason For Breaking Change**</span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><ul><li><span><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;">To further the effort of creating parity across all of our government clouds, there are certain startup modals that simply don't work inside airgapped spaces. To avoid parity conflicts we can identify if a user's tenant is eligible for one of these exclusive clouds and, if so, hide the incompatible modals on the public cloud. This maintains parity across public and government clouds for those users and thereby adheres to the parity requirement.</span></div></span></li></ul><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"></span></div><div style="box-sizing:border-box;"><span style="box-sizing:border-box;"><br></span></div></span></div><div></p></td></tr></table>
